__Nosocomial pneumonia caused by methicillin-resistant Staphylococcus aureus treated with linezolid or vancomycin: A secondary economic analysis of resource use from a Spanish perspective__

__[Nosocomial pneumonia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0949083)__  caused by __[methicillin-resistant Staphylococcus aureus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1265292)__  __[treated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  or __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__ : A secondary __[economic analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680954)__  of __[resource use](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704738)__  from a __[Spanish](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037747)__  __[perspective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680951)__ 
Adopting a unique __[Spanish](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037747)__  __[perspective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680951)__ , this __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  aims to assess __[healthcare resource utilization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704738)__  (__[HCRU](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704738)__ ) and the __[costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  of __[treating](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522326)__  __[nosocomial pneumonia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0949083)__  (__[NP](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0949083)__ ) produced by __[methicillin-resistant Staphylococcus aureus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1265292)__  (__[MRSA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1265292)__ ) in __[hospitalized adults](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0701159)__  using __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  or __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__ . An evaluation is also made of the __[renal failure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035078)__  __[rate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521828)__  and related __[economic outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1274040)__  between __[study groups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__ . An economic __[post hoc evaluation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254363)__  of a __[randomized](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2986910)__ , __[double-blind](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013072)__ , __[multicenter phase 4 study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282462)__  was carried out. __[Nosocomial pneumonia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0949083)__  due to __[MRSA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1265292)__  in __[hospitalized adults](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0701159)__ . The __[modified intent to treat](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292734)__  (__[mITT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292734)__ ) __[population](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  comprised 224 __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  - and 224 __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__  - __[treated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  and __[HCRU](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704738)__  were evaluated between __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[administered](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521801)__  either __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  or __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__ , and between __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  who developed __[renal failure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035078)__  and those who did not. Analysis of __[HCRU](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704738)__  __[outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1274040)__  and __[costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__ . Total __[costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  were similar between the __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  - (€17,782±€9,615) and __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__  - __[treated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (€17,423±€9,460) (P=.69). The __[renal failure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035078)__  __[rate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521828)__  was significantly lower in the __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  - __[treated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (4% vs. 15%; P<.001). The total __[costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  tended to be higher in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  who developed __[renal failure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035078)__  (€19,626±€10,840 vs. €17,388±€9,369; P=.14). Among the __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  who developed __[renal failure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035078)__ , __[HCRU](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704738)__  (__[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  on __[mechanical ventilation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0199470)__ : 13.2±10.7 vs. 7.6±3.6 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ ; P=.21; __[ICU stay](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__ : 14.4±10.5 vs. 9.9±6.6 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ ; P=.30; __[hospital stay](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3489408)__ : 19.5±9.5 vs. 16.1±11.0 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ ; P=.26) and __[cost](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  (€17,219±€8,792 vs. €20,263±€11,350; P=.51) tended to be lower in the __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  - vs. __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__  - __[treated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . There were no statistically significant differences in __[costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  per __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  - __[day](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  between __[cohorts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599755)__  after correcting for __[mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__  (€1000 vs. €1,010; P=.98). From a __[Spanish](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037747)__  __[perspective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680951)__ , there were no statistically significant differences in total __[costs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085552)__  between the __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  and __[vancomycin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042313)__  __[pneumonia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032285)__  __[cohorts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599755)__ . The __[drug cost](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085123)__  corresponding to __[linezolid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0663241)__  was partially __[offset](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1711330)__  by fewer __[renal failure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035078)__  __[adverse events](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0877248)__ 

* * *

__The Role of TRAF4 and B3GAT1 Gene Expression in the Food Hypersensitivity and Insect Venom Allergy in Mastocytosis__

The Role of __[TRAF4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1336665)__  and __[B3GAT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412716)__  __[Gene Expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  in the __[Food Hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016470)__  and __[Insect Venom Allergy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020517)__  in __[Mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__ 
__[Mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  is an uncommon __[disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012634)__  classified as a __[myeloproliferative neoplasm](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027022)__ , however, its __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__  are broad and place __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  at crossroads between __[dermatology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011627)__ , __[hematology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018943)__  and allergology. __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  often suffer from __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__  resulting from the __[activation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1879547)__  and release of mediators from the __[mast cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024880)__ , such as generalized __[itching](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033774)__ , __[redness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0041834)__ , __[headache](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018681)__ , __[abdominal cramps](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000729)__ , __[diarrhea](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011991)__ , __[bone pain](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0151825)__  or __[arthritis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003864)__ , __[hypotension](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020649)__  and __[shock](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036974)__ . The possible severe, __[fatal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1302234)__  or near __[fatal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1302234)__  reactions caused by __[food hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016470)__  are reasons for the research focused on __[marker](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005516)__  identification. The aim of the __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  was to analyse the __[gene expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  differences in __[mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with and without __[food](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016470)__  and __[drug hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013182)__  and __[insect venom allergy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020517)__  (__[IVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020517)__ ). A total of 57 __[Caucasian](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043157)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  were studied [median __[age](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__  41.8; range 18-77 __[years](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439234)__ ; 15 (26.3 %) __[males](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086582)__  and 42 (73.7 %) __[females](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086287)__ ]. __[Quantitative RT-PCRs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3179034)__  of 11 __[genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017337)__  plus __[ribosomal 18S RNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035703)__  were run. __[Symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__  of __[food hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016470)__  were found in 12 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (21 %), including 3 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (13 %) with __[cutaneous mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1136033)__  (__[CM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1136033)__ ), and 9 (28 %) with __[indolent systemic mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0272203)__  (__[ISM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0272203)__ ). __[IVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020517)__  was confirmed in 13 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (22.8 %) including 6 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (10.5 %) with __[CM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1136033)__ , and 7 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (12.3 %) with __[ISM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0272203)__ . __[Drug hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013182)__  was __[diagnosed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  in 10 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (17.5 %). Significant differences in the __[gene expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  were found for __[TRAF4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1336665)__  (p = 0.008) in the comparison of the __[mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with and without concomitant __[food hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016470)__ . Furthermore significant differences were found in __[gene expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  for __[B3GAT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412716)__  (p = 0.003) in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[IVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020517)__  compared to __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  without __[insect sting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079626)__  __[anaphylaxis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002792)__  in the medical history. The __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  of studied __[genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017337)__  did not differ according to the presence of __[drug hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013182)__ . The __[TRAF4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1336665)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  was higher in __[mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[food hypersensitivity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016470)__  in their __[medical history](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0262926)__ , the __[B3GAT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412716)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  was lower in __[mastocytosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024899)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[IVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020517)__ 

* * *

__Generalized Weakness in a Transplant Patient: A Case Presentation__

__[Generalized Weakness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714552)__  in a __[Transplant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3841811)__  __[Patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ : A __[Case Presentation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085973)__ 
__[Generalized weakness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714552)__  in __[transplant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3841811)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  is a major complaint in tertiary __[rehabilitation hospitals](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0337962)__ . The __[diagnosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  and __[management](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1536570)__  of __[generalized weakness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714552)__  in this __[population](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  pose challenges for __[physicians](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031831)__ . We present the case of a __[transplant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3841811)__  __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[generalized weakness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714552)__  who was eventually __[diagnosed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  with __[calciphylaxis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006666)__  using a __[multidisciplinary diagnostic approach](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0729737)__  of __[electrodiagnostics](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013816)__ , __[vascular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005847)__  __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086143)__ , and __[skin biopsy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0150866)__ . __[Calciphylaxis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006666)__  is a rare __[cutaneous disorder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037274)__  that mimics other __[collagen vascular diseases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0262428)__  in its presentation and fulminant course. __[Physiatrists](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0260138)__  should be cognizant of __[calciphylaxis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006666)__ , as it signals a __[poor prognosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0278252)__  if not __[correctly diagnosed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  and __[treated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522326)__  in a __[timely manner](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3827828)__ , with high __[incidence](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021149)__  of __[sepsis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243026)__ , __[wound pain](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241745)__ , and __[disability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0231170)__ 

* * *

__Use of ecoacoustics to determine biodiversity patterns across ecological gradients__

Use of __[ecoacoustics](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242479)__  to determine __[biodiversity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282469)__  __[patterns](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449774)__  across __[ecological](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0565987)__  __[gradients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0812409)__ 
The variety of __[local](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205276)__  __[animal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003062)__  __[sounds](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037709)__  __[characterizes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3875152)__  a __[landscape](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870781)__ . We used __[ecoacoustics](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242479)__  to noninvasively __[assess](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  the __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__  richness of __[various](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439064)__  __[biotopes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__  typical of an __[ecofriendly forest plantation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086312)__  with __[diverse](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1880371)__  __[ecological](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0565987)__  __[gradients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0812409)__  and both __[nonnative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2230122)__  and __[indigenous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512704)__  __[vegetation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032098)__ . The __[reference](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1706462)__  __[area](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__  was an __[adjacent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205117)__  large __[World Heritage Site protected area](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__  (__[PA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__ ). All __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  were in a __[global biodiversity hotspot](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__ . Our __[results](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1274040)__  showed how __[taxa](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1515221)__  __[segregated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443299)__  into __[various](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439064)__  __[biotopes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__ . We __[identified](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205396)__  65 __[singing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042932)__  __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__ , including __[birds](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005595)__ , __[frogs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003459)__ , __[crickets](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018288)__ , and __[katydids](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0684063)__ . __[Large](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0549177)__ , __[natural](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205296)__ , protected __[grassland sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442534)__  in the __[PA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__  had the __[highest](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522410)__  __[mean acoustic diversity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__  (14.1 __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__  / __[site](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__ ). __[Areas](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205146)__  covered in __[nonnative timber](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032098)__  or __[grass](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018210)__  __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__  were devoid of __[acoustic species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__ . __[Sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  grazed by __[native](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0302891)__  and __[domestic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1880391)__  __[megaherbivores](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0562691)__  were fairly rich (5.1) in __[acoustic species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__  but none were __[unique](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1710548)__  to this __[habitat type](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871648)__ , where __[acoustic diversity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1880371)__  was greater than in intensively managed __[grassland](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442534)__  __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  (0.04). __[Natural vegetation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086312)__  patches inside the __[plantation mosaic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  supported high __[mean acoustic diversity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__  (__[indigenous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512704)__  __[forests](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086312)__  7.6, __[grasslands](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442534)__  8.0, __[wetlands](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1721088)__  9.1), which increased as __[plant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032098)__  __[heterogeneity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019409)__  and __[patch size](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449456)__  __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__ . __[Indigenous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512704)__  __[forest patches](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086312)__  within the __[plantation mosaic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  contained a highly __[characteristic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521970)__  __[acoustic species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__  __[assemblage](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254370)__ , emphasizing their complementary __[contribution](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1880177)__  to __[local](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205276)__  __[biodiversity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282469)__ . Overall, __[acoustic signals](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0028263)__  determined spatial __[biodiversity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282469)__  __[patterns](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449774)__  and can be a useful tool for guiding __[conservation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347858)__ 

* * *

__A Randomized Controlled Noninferiority Trial of Single Dose of Oral Dexamethasone Versus 5 Days of Oral Prednisone in Acute Adult Asthma__

A __[Randomized Controlled Noninferiority Trial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206035)__  of __[Single Dose](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178602)__  of __[Oral Dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0360528)__  Versus 5 __[Days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  of __[Oral Prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3216040)__  in Acute __[Adult](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001675)__  __[Asthma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004096)__ 
__[Oral dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0360528)__  __[demonstrates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3687625)__  __[bioavailability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005508)__  __[similar](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348205)__  to that of __[oral prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3216040)__  but has a longer __[half-life](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018517)__ . We evaluate whether a __[single dose](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178602)__  of __[oral dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0360528)__  __[plus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332287)__  4 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  of __[placebo](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1696465)__  is not __[inferior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0542339)__  to 5 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  of __[oral prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3216040)__  in __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522326)__  of __[adults](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001675)__  with __[mild](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0581124)__  to __[moderate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0581125)__  __[asthma exacerbations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0349790)__  to __[prevent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292733)__  __[relapse](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035020)__  defined as an __[unscheduled](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3854240)__  return visit for __[additional treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1706712)__  for __[persistent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3266628)__  or __[worsening](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332271)__  __[asthma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004096)__  within 14 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ . __[Adult](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001675)__  __[emergency department](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3840745)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (__[aged](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__  18 to 55 __[years](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439234)__ ) were __[randomized](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034656)__  to __[receive](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514756)__  either a __[single dose](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178602)__  of 12 mg of __[oral dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0360528)__  with 4 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  of __[placebo](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1696465)__  or a 5- __[day](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  __[course](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0750729)__  of __[oral prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3216040)__  60 mg a __[day](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ . __[Outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1274040)__  __[including](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332257)__  __[relapse](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035020)__  were __[assessed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516048)__  by a __[follow-up telephone interview](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178941)__  at 2 __[weeks](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439230)__ . One __[hundred seventy-three](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__  __[dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011777)__  and 203 __[prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032952)__  __[subjects](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681850)__  __[completed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205197)__  the study regimen and __[telephone follow-up](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178941)__ . The __[dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011777)__  __[group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  by a small margin surpassed the preset 8% __[difference](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705242)__  between __[groups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  for __[noninferiority](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  in __[relapse](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035020)__  __[rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521828)__  within 14 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  (12.1% versus 9.8%; __[difference](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705242)__  2.3%; 95% __[confidence interval](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009667)__  -4.1% to 8.6%). __[Subjects](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681850)__  in the 2 __[groups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  had similar __[rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521828)__  of __[hospitalization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019993)__  for their __[relapse](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035020)__  __[visit](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512346)__  (__[dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011777)__  3.4% versus __[prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032952)__  2.9%; __[difference](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705242)__  0.5%; 95% __[confidence interval](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009667)__  -4.1% to 3.1%). __[Adverse effect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280500)__  __[rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521828)__  were generally the same in the 2 __[groups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__ . A __[single dose](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178602)__  of __[oral dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0360528)__  did not __[demonstrate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3687625)__  __[noninferiority](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  to __[prednisone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032952)__  for 5 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  by a very small margin for __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522326)__  of __[adults](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001675)__  with __[mild](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0581124)__  to __[moderate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0581125)__  __[asthma exacerbations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0349790)__ . __[Enhanced](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2349975)__  __[compliance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714738)__  and __[convenience](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3831015)__  may support the __[use](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0457083)__  of __[dexamethasone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011777)__ 

* * *

__Relationship between XspI Site Polymorphisms of LDL-R Gene and Serum IL-2 and IL-10 in Patients with Hypercholesterolemia__

__[Relationship](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  between __[XspI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0752931)__  __[Site Polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1709929)__  of __[LDL-R Gene](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  and __[Serum IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__  and __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__  in __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[Hypercholesterolemia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020443)__ 
__[Relationship](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  has been __[identified](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205396)__  in __[sporadic reports](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  between __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  and __[hypercholesterolemia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020443)__ . However, the __[relationship](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  between __[inflammatory](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0333348)__  __[cytokines](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079189)__  and __[polymorphism](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  of __[low-density lipoprotein receptor (LDL-R) gene](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  in __[hypercholesterolemia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020443)__  is __[unclear](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3845108)__ . This __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  __[aimed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1947946)__  to explore the __[relationship](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  and __[significance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0750502)__  between __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  of __[LDL-R gene](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  and __[serum Interleukin-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__  (__[IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__ ), __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[hypercholesterolemia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020443)__ . __[PCR-RFLP](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0200930)__  and __[direct DNA sequencing assay](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0917792)__  were __[employed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0557351)__  to determine __[polymorphism](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  of __[LDL-R gene](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  in 900 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[hypercholesterolemia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020443)__  and 400 __[healthy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3898900)__  __[cases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0868928)__ . __[ELISA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014441)__  was __[applied](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4048755)__  to __[assay serum concentration](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683149)__  of __[IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__  and __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__ . __[Blood lipid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596192)__  __[indexes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600653)__  were __[tested](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039593)__  in all __[cases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0868928)__ . __[Compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  with the __[healthy controls](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2986479)__ , __[level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  of __[IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__  __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[significantly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0750502)__ , while __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__  __[decreased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205216)__  __[significantly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0750502)__  (P < 0.05). __[Correlation analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010101)__  showed that __[IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__  was __[positively](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3843166)__  __[correlated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  with __[total cholesterol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543421)__  (__[TC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543421)__ ), __[LDL-c](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023824)__ , and __[genotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__  (r = 0.542, 0.410, 0.598, P < 0.05) and __[negatively](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  __[correlated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  with __[HDL-c](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023822)__  (r = -0.352, P < 0.05). __[Negative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205160)__  __[relationship](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  also was found between __[TC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543421)__ , __[LDL-c](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023824)__ , __[genotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__ , and __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__  (r = -0.452, -0.390, -0.613, P < 0.05), and __[positive](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1446409)__  __[correlation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  between __[HDL-c](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023822)__  and __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__  (r = 0.398, P < 0.05). __[Multiple linear regression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023733)__  showed that __[genotypes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__  and __[TC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543421)__  were __[independent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085862)__  __[factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521761)__  __[affecting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392760)__  the __[levels of IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022885)__  and __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022885)__  (P < 0.05). __[IL-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021756)__  and __[IL-10](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085295)__  were __[related](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  to __[gene polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  of __[LDL-R](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__ , which might be __[involved](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1314939)__  in the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  and __[progress](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280477)__  of __[hypercholesterolemia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020443)__ 

* * *

__HERG1 potassium channel expression in potentially malignant disorders of the oral mucosa and prognostic relevance in oral squamous cell carcinoma__

__[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[potassium channel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032824)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  in __[potentially](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3245505)__  __[malignant disorders](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006826)__  of the __[oral mucosa](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026639)__  and __[prognostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220901)__  __[relevance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347946)__  in __[oral squamous cell carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__ 
__[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[potassium channel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032824)__  plays a __[critical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1511545)__  __[role](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705810)__  in the __[cell proliferation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596290)__ . __[HERG1 protein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  was __[analyzed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0936012)__  by __[immunohistochemistry](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021044)__  (__[IHC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021044)__ ) in 62 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[oral leukoplakias](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023532)__  and 100 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[oral squamous cell carcinomas](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__  (__[OSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__ ). __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1416571)__  __[mRNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035696)__  __[levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  were __[assessed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516048)__  by __[real-time reverse transcriptase-polymerase chain reaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599161)__  (__[RT-PCR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599161)__ ) in 22 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[primary](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205225)__  __[head and neck squamous cell carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1168401)__  (__[HNSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1168401)__ ). __[Statistically significant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237881)__  __[associations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  were found between __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  and __[tobacco consumption](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543414)__ , __[disease stage](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0699749)__ , __[tumor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027651)__  __[differentiation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007589)__ , __[tumor recurrence](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521158)__ , and __[reduced](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392756)__  __[survival](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038952)__ . There was __[no](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1518422)__  __[association](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  between __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  and the __[risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035647)__  of __[progression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178874)__  from __[oral leukoplakia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023532)__  to __[OSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__ . In addition, a __[high](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205250)__  __[proportion](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1709707)__  of __[tumors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027651)__  (80%) showed __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1416571)__  __[mRNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035696)__  __[levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  to __[normal mucosa](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026724)__  from __[nononcologic patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Aberrant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443127)__  __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  __[increases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442805)__  as oral __[tumorigenesis progresses](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178874)__  from __[oral hyperplasia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1400010)__  to __[OSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__ . __[Increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1416571)__  __[mRNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035696)__  __[levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  were also frequently __[detected](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442726)__  in __[OSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__  and other __[HNSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1168401)__  __[subsites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1710234)__ . __[HERG1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1566128)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  emerges as a __[clinically](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[relevant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347946)__  __[feature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348519)__  during __[tumor progression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178874)__  and a __[potential](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3245505)__  __[poor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2700379)__  __[prognostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220901)__  __[biomarker](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005516)__  for __[OSCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0585362)__

__Malignancy is associated with microcalcification and higher AP/T ratio in ultrasonography, but not with Hashimoto's thyroiditis in histopathology in patients with thyroid nodules evaluated as Bethesda Category III (AUS / FLUS) in cytology__

__[Malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  is __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  __[microcalcification](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521174)__  and __[higher AP/T ratio](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456603)__  in __[ultrasonography](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0041618)__ , but not with __[Hashimoto's thyroiditis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0677607)__  in __[histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430445)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[thyroid nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  evaluated as __[Bethesda Category III](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  (__[AUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522580)__  / __[FLUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272585)__ ) in __[cytology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1305671)__ 
The __[predictors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683956)__  of __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  are important for the decision of appropriate __[management](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0376636)__  in __[nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  with __[atypia of undetermined significance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522580)__  / __[follicular lesion of undetermined significance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272585)__  (__[AUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522580)__  / __[FLUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272585)__ ). Our aim was to determine the __[ultrasonographical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683956)__ , __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683956)__ , and __[biochemical predictors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683956)__  of __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  in these __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . A total of 427 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[cytologically Bethesda Category III](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  (__[AUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522580)__  / __[FLUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272585)__ ) __[thyroid nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  were included in this __[retrospective study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035363)__ . We divided the __[nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  into two __[subgroups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  according to the __[histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430445)__  as __[benign](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205183)__  and __[malignant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205282)__ , and compared the __[preoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0445204)__  __[ultrasonographical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1720195)__ , __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3854293)__ , and __[biochemical findings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__ . In overall, 427 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with 449 __[AUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522580)__  / __[FLUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272585)__  __[nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  who had undergone __[surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543467)__ , the rate of __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  was 23.4 % (105/449). When evaluated separately, the rate of __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  was 25.8 % in __[nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  with __[AUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522580)__  (82/318) and 17.6 % in __[nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  with __[FLUS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272585)__  (23/131) (p = 0.061). The vast majority of __[malignant specimens](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347026)__  in __[histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430445)__  consisted of __[papillary thyroid carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0238463)__  (__[PTC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0238463)__ ) (n = 91, 86.7 %). __[Preoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0445204)__  __[ultrasonographic features](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1720195)__  of 105 __[malignant nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  in __[histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430445)__  were compared with the 344 __[benign nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0749467)__  in __[histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430445)__ . __[Anteroposterior/Transverse (AP/T) ratio](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456603)__  was significantly higher in __[malignant group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  compared to __[benign group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  (p = 0.013). In __[multiple logistic analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0936012)__ , we found that __[higher AP/T ratio](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456603)__  and __[microcalcification](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521174)__  were independently __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  (p < 0.05). The __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  -associated cut-off value of __[AP/T ratio](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456603)__  at maximum __[sensitivity and specificity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036668)__  was ≥0.81. We did not find any __[correlation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  between __[malignancy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  and __[Hashimoto's thyroiditis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0677607)__  in __[histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430445)__  in __[multivariate analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026777)__  (p > 0.05). In __[Bethesda Category III nodules](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040137)__  with __[higher AP/T ratio](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456603)__  and __[microcalcification](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521174)__ , __[surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543467)__  might be considered as a first therapeutic option instead of repeat __[fine-needle aspiration biopsy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1510483)__  or __[observation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0302523)__ 

* * *

__Low serum vitamin D is associated with higher cortical porosity in elderly men__

__[Low](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205251)__  __[serum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229671)__  __[vitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042866)__  is __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  higher __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[porosity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080037)__  in __[elderly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001792)__  __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__ 
__[Bone loss](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029453)__  at __[peripheral](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205100)__  __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1515974)__  in the __[elderly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001792)__  is mainly __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  and involves __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[porosity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080037)__ . However, an __[association](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  between __[bone loss](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029453)__  at these __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1515974)__  and __[25-hydroxyvitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0535968)__  has not been reported. To __[investigate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__  the __[association](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439849)__  between __[serum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229671)__  __[levels of 25-hydroxyvitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2984945)__ , __[bone microstructure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0262950)__  and __[areal bone mineral density](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__  (__[BMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__ ) in __[elderly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001792)__  __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__ . A __[population](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  -based __[cohort](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599755)__  of 444 __[elderly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001792)__  __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__  (mean ± SD __[age](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__  80.2 ± 3.5 __[years](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1510829)__ ) was __[investigated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__ . __[Bone microstructure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0262950)__  was measured by __[high-resolution peripheral quantitative computed tomography](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040405)__ , __[areal BMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__  by __[dual-energy X-ray absorptiometry](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1510486)__  and __[serum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229671)__  __[25-hydroxyvitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2984945)__  and __[parathyroid hormone levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0202159)__  by __[immunoassay](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020980)__ . __[Mean](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0444504)__  __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[porosity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080037)__  at the __[distal tibia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0588200)__  was 14.7% higher (12.5 ± 4.3% vs. 10.9 ± 4.1%, P < 0.05) whilst __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[volumetric BMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__ , __[area](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205146)__ , __[trabecular bone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222660)__  __[volume fraction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0560268)__  and __[femoral neck](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0015815)__  __[areal BMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__  were lower in __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__  in the lowest __[quartile](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2828255)__  of __[vitamin D levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0919758)__  compared to the highest. In __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__  with __[vitamin D deficiency](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042870)__  (<25 nmol L(-1)) or __[insufficiency](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0231179)__  [25-49 nmol L(-1), in combination with an __[elevated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3163633)__  __[serum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229671)__  __[level of parathyroid hormone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0202159)__  (>6.8 pmol L(-1))], __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[porosity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080037)__  was 17.2% higher than in __[vitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042866)__  - __[sufficient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205410)__  __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__  (P < 0.01). A __[linear regression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023733)__  __[model](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3161035)__  including __[age](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__ , __[weight](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005910)__ , __[height](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005890)__ , __[daily calcium intake](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2183363)__ , __[physical activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026606)__ , __[smoking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037369)__  __[vitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042866)__  __[supplementation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0302837)__  and __[parathyroid hormone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030520)__  showed that __[25-hydroxyvitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0535968)__  independently predicted __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[porosity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080037)__  (standardized β = -0.110, R(2) = 1.1%, P = 0.024), __[area](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205146)__  (β = 0.123, R(2) = 1.4%, P = 0.007) and __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[volumetric BMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__  (β = 0.125, R(2) = 1.4%, P = 0.007) of the __[tibia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040184)__  as well as __[areal BMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__  of the __[femoral neck](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0015815)__  (β = 0.102, R(2) = 0.9%, P = 0.04). __[Serum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229671)__  __[vitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042866)__  is __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[porosity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080037)__ , __[area](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205146)__  and __[density](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005938)__ , indicating that __[bone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0262950)__  __[fragility](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0302113)__  as a result of __[low](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205251)__  __[vitamin D](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042866)__  could be due to __[changes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392747)__  in __[cortical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0222652)__  __[bone microstructure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0262950)__  and __[geometry](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678594)__
