__Nationwide reduction in the number of corneal transplantations for keratoconus following the implementation of cross-linking__

__[Nationwide](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  __[reduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547047)__  in the number of __[corneal transplantations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  for __[keratoconus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022578)__  following the __[implementation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1708476)__  of __[cross-linking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__ 
__[Keratoconus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022578)__  is characterized by __[corneal ectasia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0155135)__  and __[irregular astigmatism](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0152194)__ , which can lead to __[diminished vision](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042798)__  and __[corneal scarring](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0349702)__ . Approximately 10-20% of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[keratoconus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022578)__  eventually require a __[corneal transplant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__ . __[Corneal cross-linking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__  (__[CXL](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__ ) is a relatively new __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  that may help prevent the need for __[corneal transplantation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__ . Here, we __[investigated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__  whether the __[introduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0579004)__  of __[CXL](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__  has reduced the number of __[corneal transplants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  __[annually](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332181)__ . __[Data](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1511726)__  regarding the __[transplantation procedures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040732)__  __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  under the __[age](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__  of 50 __[years](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439234)__  were extracted from the __[Dutch National Organ Transplant Registry](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034975)__ . The number of __[corneal transplants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  prior to (i.e. in 2005 through 2007) and following the __[introduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0579004)__  of __[CXL](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__  (i.e. in 2012 through 2014) were __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__ . Furthermore, a __[trend analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681702)__  on __[annual](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332181)__  __[keratoplasties](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  over time was __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__ . Approximately 25% fewer __[corneal transplants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  were __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  in the 3- __[year](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439234)__  period following the __[introduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0579004)__  of __[CXL](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__  __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  to the 3- __[year](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439234)__  period prior to the __[introduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0579004)__  of __[CXL](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__  (201 versus 269 __[transplants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__ , respectively; p = 0.005). __[Age](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__ , __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__  and __[visual acuity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042812)__  were similar between the __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  groups in the two __[time periods](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1948053)__ . __[Trend analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681702)__  also demonstrated a significant __[decrease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547047)__  in the amount of __[corneal transplants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  (p = 0.001). Significantly fewer __[corneal transplants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__  were performed for treating __[keratoconus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022578)__  following the __[nationwide](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  __[introduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0579004)__  of __[CXL](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__ . This __[reduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547047)__  suggests that __[corneal cross-linking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4065848)__  can significantly __[reduce](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392756)__  the need for __[corneal transplantation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010042)__ 

* * *

__Rapid Fabrication of a Cell - Seeded Collagen Gel -Based Tubular Construct that Withstands Arterial Pressure: Rapid Fabrication of a Gel -Based Media Equivalent__

Rapid __[Fabrication](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  of a __[Cell](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  - __[Seeded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3828225)__  __[Collagen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009325)__  __[Gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  -Based __[Tubular Construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  that Withstands __[Arterial Pressure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0232108)__ : Rapid __[Fabrication](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  of a __[Gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  -Based __[Media](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705217)__  Equivalent
Based on __[plastically compressed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728907)__  __[cell](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  - __[seeded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3828225)__  __[collagen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009325)__  __[gels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__ , we __[fabricated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  a small-diameter __[tubular construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  that withstands __[arterial pressure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0232108)__  without prolonged __[culture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0430400)__  __[in vitro](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1533691)__ . Specifically, to mimic the __[microstructure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678594)__  of __[vascular media](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162867)__ , the __[cell](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  - __[seeded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3828225)__  __[collagen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009325)__  __[gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  was uniaxially stretched prior to __[plastic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032167)__  __[compression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728907)__  to align __[collagen fibers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0225325)__  and hence __[cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  in the __[gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__ . The resulting __[gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  __[sheet](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005479)__  was then wrapped around a custom-made __[multi-layered braided tube](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184166)__  to form aligned __[tubular constructs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  whereas the __[gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  __[sheet](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005479)__  prepared similarly but without uniaxial stretching formed control __[constructs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__ . With the __[braided tube](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184166)__ , __[fluid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704353)__  in the __[gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  __[construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  was further removed by __[vacuum suction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0182957)__  aiming to consolidate the concentric layers of the __[construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__ . The __[construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  was finally treated with __[transglutaminase](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033679)__ . Both __[SEM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026020)__  and __[histology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0344441)__  confirmed the absence of gaps in the wall of the __[construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__ . Particularly, __[cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  in the wall of the aligned __[tubular construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  were circumferentially aligned. The __[enzyme](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014442)__  -mediated __[crosslinking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178576)__  increased __[burst pressure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033095)__  of both the __[constructs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  significantly; the extent of the increase of __[burst pressure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033095)__  for the aligned __[tubular construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  was greater than that for the control counterpart. Increasing __[crosslinking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178576)__  left the compliance of the aligned __[tubular construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  unchanged but reduced that of the control __[construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__ . __[Cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  remained viable in __[transglutaminase](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033679)__  -treated __[plastically compressed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728907)__  __[gels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  after 6 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  in culture. This __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  demonstrated that by combining stretch-induced __[fiber](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0225325)__  __[alignment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1706765)__ , __[plastic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032167)__  __[compression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728907)__ , and __[enzyme](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014442)__  -mediated __[crosslinking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178576)__ , a __[cell](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  - __[seeded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3828225)__  __[collagen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009325)__  __[gel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017243)__  -based __[tubular construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175730)__  with potential to be used as __[vascular media](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162867)__  can be made within 3 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ 

* * *

__Impact of cofactor - binding loop mutations on thermotolerance and activity of E. coli transketolase__

__[Impact](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049986)__  of __[cofactor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178555)__  - __[binding loop](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0682969)__  __[mutations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026882)__  on __[thermotolerance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3544386)__  and __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243102)__  of __[E. coli](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014834)__  __[transketolase](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040709)__ 
__[Improvement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2986411)__  of __[thermostability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597571)__  in __[engineered enzymes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014442)__  can allow __[biocatalysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2350294)__  on __[substrates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3891814)__  with poor __[aqueous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599956)__  __[solubility](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037628)__ . __[Denaturation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033627)__  of the __[cofactor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178555)__  - __[binding loops](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0682969)__  of __[Escherichia coli](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014834)__  __[transketolase](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040709)__  (__[TK](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040709)__ ) was previously linked to the __[loss](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1517945)__  of __[enzyme activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243102)__  under __[conditions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0348080)__  of __[high](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205250)__  __[pH](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020283)__  or __[urea](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0041942)__ . __[Incubation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022885)__  at __[temperatures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  just below the __[thermal melting transition](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254365)__ , above which the __[protein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033684)__  __[aggregates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332621)__ , was also found to __[anneal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  the __[enzyme](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014442)__  to give an __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  specific __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243102)__ . The potential __[role](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705810)__  of __[cofactor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178555)__  - __[binding loop](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0682969)__  __[instability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1444783)__  in this process remained unclear. In this work, the two __[cofactor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0178555)__  - __[binding loops](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0682969)__  (__[residues 185-192](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002518)__  and __[382-392](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002518)__ ) were progressively mutated towards the equivalent __[sequence](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004793)__  from the __[thermostable](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  __[Thermus thermophilus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085475)__  __[TK](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040709)__  and __[variants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678941)__  __[assessed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516048)__  for their __[impact](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049986)__  on both __[thermostability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597571)__  and __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__ . __[Cofactor-binding loop 2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004793)__  __[variants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678941)__  had __[detrimental effects](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280500)__  on specific __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  at __[elevated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3163633)__  __[temperatures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__ , whereas the __[H192P mutation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026882)__  in __[cofactor-binding loop 1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004793)__  resulted in a two-fold improved __[stability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597571)__  to __[inactivation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0544461)__  at __[elevated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3163633)__  __[temperatures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__ , and __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  the __[critical onset temperature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  for __[aggregation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332621)__ . The specific __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  of __[H192P](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026882)__  was 3-fold and 19-fold __[higher](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205250)__  than that for __[wild-type](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1883559)__  at 60°C and 65°C respectively, and also remained 2.7-4 fold __[higher](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205250)__  after __[re-cooling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678568)__  from __[pre-incubations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022885)__  at either 55°C or 60°C for 1h. Interestingly, __[H192P](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026882)__  was also 2-times more __[active](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205177)__  than __[wild-type](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1883559)__  __[TK](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040709)__  at 25°C. __[Optimal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2698651)__  __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  was achieved at 60°C for __[H192P](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026882)__  compared to 55°C for __[wild type](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1883559)__ . These results show that __[cofactor-binding loop 1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004793)__ , plays a pivotal __[role](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705810)__  in __[partial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728938)__  __[denaturation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033627)__  and __[aggregation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332621)__  at __[elevated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3163633)__  __[temperatures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__ . Furthermore, a __[single rigidifying mutation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026882)__  within this __[loop](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004793)__  can significantly improve the __[enzyme specific activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243102)__ , as well as the __[stability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597571)__  to __[thermal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018837)__  __[denaturation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033627)__  and __[aggregation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332621)__ , to give an __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[temperature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  __[optimum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2698651)__  for __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243102)__ 

* * *

__Expression and Purification of E2 Glycoprotein from Insect Cells (Sf9) for Use in Serology__

__[Expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  and __[Purification](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597301)__  of __[E2 Glycoprotein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017968)__  from __[Insect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021585)__  __[Cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  (__[Sf9](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3494245)__ ) for Use in __[Serology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036743)__ 
__[Chikungunya virus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008056)__  (__[CHIKV](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008056)__ ) is a __[mosquito](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026584)__  - __[borne](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0699809)__  __[arbovirus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003725)__  which poses a major __[threat](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0749385)__  to __[global](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348867)__  __[public health](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0699943)__ . __[Definitive](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443196)__  __[CHIKV](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008056)__  __[diagnosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  is crucial, especially in distinguishing the __[disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012634)__  from __[dengue virus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011315)__ , which __[co-circulates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175630)__  in __[endemic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  __[areas](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205146)__  and shares the same __[mosquito vectors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4277713)__ . __[Laboratory diagnosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011911)__  is mainly __[based](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527178)__  on __[serological](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220911)__  or __[molecular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521991)__  approaches. The __[E2 glycoprotein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017968)__  is a good candidate for __[serological diagnosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036743)__  since it is the __[immunodominant antigen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0078968)__  __[during](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0347984)__  the __[course](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0750729)__  of __[infection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714514)__ , and __[reacts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443286)__  with __[seropositive](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521143)__  __[CHIKV](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008056)__  __[sera](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229671)__ . In this __[chapter](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1552857)__ , we __[describe](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1552738)__  the __[generation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3146294)__  of __[stable](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205360)__  __[clone](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009013)__  __[Sf9](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3494245)__  (__[Spodoptera frugiperda](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242626)__ ) __[cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009013)__  __[expressing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  __[secreted](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1327616)__ , __[soluble](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1749467)__ , and __[native](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0302891)__  __[recombinant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514798)__  __[CHIKV](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008056)__  __[E2 glycoprotein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017968)__ . We use direct __[plasmid](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032136)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0185117)__  in __[insect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021585)__  __[cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__ , rather than the __[traditional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443324)__  __[technique](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449851)__  of __[generating](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3146294)__  __[recombinant baculovirus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597363)__ . This __[recombinant protein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034861)__  is useful for __[serological diagnosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036743)__  of __[CHIKV](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008056)__  __[infection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714514)__ 

* * *

__Acute risk factors for suicide attempts and death: prospective findings from the STEP - BD study__

__[Acute](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205178)__  __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  for __[suicide attempts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038663)__  and __[death](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1306577)__ : __[prospective findings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033522)__  from the __[STEP](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254363)__  - __[BD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005586)__  __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__ 
__[Suicide](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038661)__  is unfortunately common in __[psychiatric](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033873)__  __[practice](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237607)__ , but difficult to __[predict](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681842)__ . The present __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  sought to __[assess](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184514)__  which __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__  __[increase](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442805)__  in the __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  before __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__  in a __[sample](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0370003)__  of __[psychiatric](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033873)__  __[outpatients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029921)__  with __[bipolar disorder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005586)__ . __[Data](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1511726)__  from the __[Systematic Treatment Enhancement Program](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254363)__  for __[Bipolar Disorder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005586)__  (__[STEP](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254363)__  - __[BD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005586)__ ) __[trial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008976)__  were used. A total of 103 __[participants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  who __[attempted suicide](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038663)__  or __[died](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4264514)__  by __[suicide](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038661)__  during the __[trial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008976)__  were included; a 15% __[random](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439605)__  __[sample](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0370003)__  of the remaining __[participants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  (n = 427) was used as a __[comparison](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  __[sample](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0370003)__ . __[Linear mixed models](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023732)__  in the six __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  before __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__  were conducted for each of five proposed __[acute](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205178)__  __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  for __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__ . __[Participants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  were __[assessed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516048)__  using the __[Clinical Monitoring Form](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516647)__  (__[CMF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516647)__ ) at each __[visit](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512346)__  for the following potential __[acute](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205178)__  __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  for __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__ : __[suicidal ideation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0424000)__ , __[loss of interest](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0424091)__ , __[anxiety](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003467)__ , __[psychomotor agitation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3887612)__ , and __[high-risk behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171309)__ . Each of the five __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__  was __[elevated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3163633)__  overall in __[individuals](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237401)__  who engaged in __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__  (p < 0.05). The __[severity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439793)__  of both __[suicidal ideation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0424000)__  and __[loss of interest](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0424091)__  significantly __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  in the __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  before __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__  (p < 0.001). __[Anxiety](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003467)__  demonstrated comparable __[effect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280500)__  __[sizes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456389)__  across __[multiple models](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3161035)__ . __[Psychomotor agitation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3887612)__  and __[high-risk behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171309)__  were not significantly __[elevated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3163633)__  before __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__ . __[Suicidal ideation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0424000)__ , __[loss of interest](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0424091)__  and, to a __[lesser](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547044)__  __[extent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439792)__ , __[anxiety](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003467)__  may represent __[acute](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205178)__  __[suicide](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038661)__  __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  up to four __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  before __[suicidal behavior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1760428)__  in __[outpatients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029921)__  with __[bipolar disorder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005586)__ . Further __[investigation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  of these potential __[acute](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205178)__  __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  in __[prospective analyses](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033522)__ 

* * *

__Measurement of Outcomes of Upper Limb Reconstructive Surgery for Tetraplegia__

__[Measurement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  of __[Outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085415)__  of __[Upper Limb Reconstructive Surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1408821)__  for __[Tetraplegia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034372)__ 
__[Reconstructive arm/hand surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1408821)__  for __[tetraplegia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034372)__  is __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  to __[improve](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184511)__  __[arm/hand function](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0562230)__  and therefore __[personal well-being](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1821407)__  for __[individuals](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237401)__  who __[accept](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272684)__  such __[elective surgeries](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206058)__ . However, __[changes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392747)__  at an __[impairment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221099)__  level do not always translate into __[functional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  or __[quality of life](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034380)__  __[changes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392747)__ . Therefore, __[multiple outcome tools](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0336791)__  should be used that __[incorporate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243126)__  __[sufficient responsiveness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3261286)__  to __[detect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442726)__  __[changes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392747)__  in __[arm/hand function](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0562230)__ , __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__  and __[participation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679823)__ , and __[quality of life](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034380)__  of the __[individuals](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237401)__  involved. This __[narrative review](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0815257)__  __[aims](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1947946)__  to __[assist](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0557034)__  __[clinicians](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871685)__  to choose the most __[appropriate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1548787)__  __[tools](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0336791)__  to __[assess](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516048)__  the need for __[reconstructive surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1408821)__  and to __[evaluate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  its __[outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085415)__ . Our specific __[objectives](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018017)__  are (1) to __[describe](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1552738)__  __[aspects](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1547011)__  to consider when choosing a __[measure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  and (2) to __[describe](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1552738)__  the __[measures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  advised by an __[international](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512888)__  __[therapist](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871525)__  consensus __[group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441833)__  __[established](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443211)__  in 2007. All advised __[measures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  are appraised in terms of the underlying __[construct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2827421)__ , __[administration](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1533734)__ , and __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[relevance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347946)__  to __[arm/hand reconstructions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0841296)__ . __[Essentially](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205224)__  there are currently no __[criterion](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243161)__  __[standard](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034925)__  __[measures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  to __[evaluate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  the __[consequences of](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0686907)__  __[reconstructive arm/hand surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1408821)__ . However, with judicious __[use](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042153)__  of available __[measures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  it is possible to ensure the __[questions asked](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0566217)__  or __[tasks](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3540678)__  __[completed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205197)__  are __[relevant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347946)__  to the __[surgical reconstruction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0524865)__  (s) undertaken. Further __[work](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043227)__  in this __[field](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521738)__  is __[required](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514873)__ . This would be best met by __[immediate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205253)__  __[collaboration](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282116)__  between 2 __[outcome's tool developers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085565)__  and by __[analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010992)__  of __[pre](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0445204)__  - and __[postoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032790)__  __[data](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1511726)__  already held in various __[international](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512888)__  sites, which would allow further __[evaluation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  of the __[measures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242485)__  already in __[use](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042153)__ , or __[components](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449432)__ 

* * *

__Basal and maximal metabolic rates differ in their response to rapid temperature change among avian species__

__[Basal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678121)__  and __[maximal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205289)__  __[metabolic rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  differ in their __[response](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871261)__  to rapid __[temperature change](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0450031)__  among __[avian](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005595)__  __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__ 
In __[birds](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005595)__ , __[acclimation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000934)__  and __[acclimatization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000934)__  to __[temperature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  are associated with changes in __[basal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678121)__  (__[BMR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678121)__ ), __[summit](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  (__[Msum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__ ) and __[maximal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205289)__  (__[MMR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__ ) __[metabolic rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  but little is known about the __[rate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  at which __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__  adjust their __[phenotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  to __[short-term](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443303)__  __[temperature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  __[variations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205419)__ . Our __[aims](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1947946)__  were (1) to determine the __[pattern](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449774)__  of __[metabolic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0311400)__  adjustments following a rapid __[temperature change](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0450031)__ , (2) to determine whether performance varies at similar __[rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  during __[exposure to](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332157)__  __[warm](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0563030)__  or __[cold environments](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241842)__ , and (3) to determine if __[BMR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678121)__ , __[Msum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  and __[MMR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  change at comparable __[rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  during __[thermal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018837)__  __[acclimation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000934)__ . We measured these parameters in __[white-throated sparrows](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1093387)__  (__[Zonotrichia albicollis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1093387)__ ), __[black-capped chickadees](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0326488)__  (__[Poecile atricapillus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0326488)__ ), and __[snow buntings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0326923)__  (__[Plectrophenax nivalis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0326923)__ ) after __[acclimation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000934)__  to 10 °C (__[day](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  0) and on the 4th and 8th __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  of __[acclimation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000934)__  to either -5 or 28 °C. __[Birds](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005595)__  changed their __[metabolic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0311400)__  __[phenotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  within 8 __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  with __[patterns](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449774)__  differing among __[species](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705920)__ . __[Sparrows](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1093387)__  expressed the expected __[metabolic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0311400)__  __[increases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442805)__  in the __[cold](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241842)__  and decreases at __[thermoneutrality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680444)__  while performance in __[chickadees](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0326488)__  and __[buntings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0326923)__  was not __[influenced](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4054723)__  by __[temperature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  but changed over time with inverse __[patterns](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449774)__ . Our __[results](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683954)__  suggest that __[BMR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678121)__  varies at comparable __[rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  in __[warm](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0563030)__  and __[cold environments](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241842)__  but changes faster than __[Msum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  and __[MMR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__ , likely due to __[limitations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449295)__  in the __[rate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870882)__  of change in __[organ size](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1450569)__  and __[function](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0542341)__ . They also suggest that __[maximal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205289)__  __[metabolic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0311400)__  __[capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516240)__  is __[lost](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0745777)__  faster in a __[warm environment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0563030)__  than it is __[gained](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1517378)__  in a __[cold environment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241842)__ . With the expected increase in __[temperature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039476)__  __[stochasticity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038347)__  at __[northern latitudes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017446)__ , a __[loss](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1517945)__  of __[thermogenic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018837)__  __[capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516240)__  during __[warm](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0563030)__  __[winter](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241737)__  __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  could, therefore, be detrimental if __[birds](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005595)__  are slow to readjust their __[phenotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  with the return of __[cold](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0241842)__  __[days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ 

* * *

__Factors preventing kneeling in a group of pre-educated patients post total knee arthroplasty__

__[Factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521761)__  __[preventing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292733)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  in a __[group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441833)__  of __[pre-educated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2106353)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[total knee arthroplasty](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ 
__[Difficulties in kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0555092)__ , one of the __[poorest scoring functional outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[total knee arthroplasty](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__  (__[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ ),have been __[attributed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449234)__  to a __[lack](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332268)__  of __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[education](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2106353)__ . This is the first study to __[investigate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__  __[specific](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205369)__  __[factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521761)__  __[affecting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392760)__  a __[patient's](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[perceived](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030971)__  __[ability to kneel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0560891)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ , following __[exposure to](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332157)__  a __[preoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0445204)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[education session](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2106353)__ . A __[cross-sectional study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010362)__  was conducted following __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__  with __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  who had been __[educated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2106353)__  about __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[prior](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332152)__  to the __[operation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543467)__ . __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  completed __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[questionnaires](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034394)__  at 6 (n = 115) and 12 (n = 82) __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ . In addition to the __[12-month](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[questionnaire](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034394)__ , __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  also completed the __[Oxford knee score](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1997265)__  (__[OKS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1997265)__ ) survey. Seventy-two __[percent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439165)__  of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[perceived](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030971)__  they could __[kneel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  at 12 __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ . Overall, __[pain](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030193)__  and __[discomfort](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2364135)__  were the most common __[factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521761)__  deterring __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  from __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__ . __[Perceived](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030971)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[ability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085732)__  was the poorest scored __[outcome](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1274040)__  on the __[OKS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1997265)__  with __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  reporting __[mild to moderate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1299392)__  __[difficulty](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0555092)__  with this task. __[Kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  scores were strongly __[correlated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  with overall __[knee function scores](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  (R = 0.70), strongly __[correlated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  with __[pain scores](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0582148)__  (R = 0.45) and weakly __[correlated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  with __[knee stability scores](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  (R = 0.29). When asked about other __[factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521761)__  __[preventing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292733)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  other than __[pain](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030193)__  or __[discomfor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2364135)__  t, 75 % had reasons __[unrelated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0445356)__  to the __[knee](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022742)__  or __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ . The most common reason was 'problems with the other __[knee](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022742)__  ' (n = 19). __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  in this study were provided with __[education](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2106353)__  regarding their __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[ability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085732)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ , yet still experienced limitations in __[perceived](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030971)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  ability __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  operatively. Contrary to previous research, our study suggests that __[factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521761)__  other than __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[education](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2106353)__  __[affect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2237113)__  a __[patient's](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[perceived](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030971)__  __[kneeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2584307)__  __[ability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085732)__  __[post](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  __[TKA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086511)__ 

* * *

__Improved diagnostic yield of neuromuscular disorders applying clinical exome sequencing in patients arising from a consanguineous population__

__[Improved](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184511)__  __[diagnostic yield](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  of __[neuromuscular disorders](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027868)__  applying __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[exome sequencing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3640077)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  arising from a __[consanguineous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680040)__  __[population](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__ 
__[Neuromuscular diseases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027868)__  (__[NMDs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027868)__ ) include a broad range of __[disorders](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012634)__  affecting __[muscles](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026845)__ , __[nerves](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027740)__  and __[neuromuscular junctions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027869)__ . Their overlapping __[phenotypes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  and __[heterogeneous genetic nature](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242960)__  have created challenges in __[diagnosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  which calls for the __[implementation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1708476)__  of __[massive parallel sequencing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2936622)__  as a candidate strategy to increase the __[diagnostic yield](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__ . In this __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__ , total of 45 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ , mostly __[offspring](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680063)__  of __[consanguineous marriages](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870340)__  were examined using __[whole exome sequencing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3640077)__ . __[Data analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0010992)__  was performed to identify the most probable __[pathogenic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3816499)__  __[rare variants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678941)__  in known __[NMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027868)__  __[genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017337)__  which led to identification of __[causal variants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205419)__  for 33 out of 45 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  (73.3%) in the following known __[genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017337)__ : __[CAPN3](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1413113)__ , __[Col6A1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1413589)__ , __[Col6A3](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1413591)__ , __[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414083)__ , __[DYSF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414209)__ , __[FHL1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414612)__ , __[GJB1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1415076)__ , __[ISPD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2829592)__ , __[LAMA2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1416776)__ , __[LMNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1416877)__ , __[PLEC1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1418643)__ , __[RYR1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419778)__ , __[SGCA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1420005)__ , __[SGCB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1420006)__ , __[SYNE1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1424736)__ , __[TNNT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1420827)__  and 22 novel __[pathogenic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3816499)__  __[variants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678941)__  were __[detected](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442726)__ . Today, the advantage of __[whole exome sequencing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3640077)__  in __[clinical diagnostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332140)__  strategies of __[heterogeneous disorders](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1858576)__  is clear. In this __[cohort](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599755)__ , a __[diagnostic yield](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  of 73.3% was achieved which is quite high __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  to the __[overall](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561607)__  reported __[diagnostic yield](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205556)__  of 25% to 50%. This could be explained by the __[consanguineous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0680040)__  background of these __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  and is another strong advantage of offering __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[exome sequencing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3640077)__  in __[diagnostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0348026)__  __[laboratories](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022877)__ , especially in __[populations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  with high rate of __[consanguinity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009789)__ 

* * *

__Safety of transradial diagnostic cardiac catheterization in patients under oral anticoagulant therapy__

__[Safety](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705187)__  of __[transradial diagnostic cardiac catheterization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2041518)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  under __[oral](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442027)__  __[anticoagulant therapy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0150457)__ 
__[Cardiac catheterization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018795)__  in __[anticoagulated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0741134)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  is usually __[performed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  after the __[anticoagulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003281)__  has been __[withdrawn](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707825)__ , at least in the previous 48h, and sometimes __[bridging therapy with heparin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3873426)__  is used. A prospective __[observational study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1518527)__  including 489 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  undergoing __[transradial catheterization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018795)__  was conducted. A total of 140 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  were under __[acenocoumarol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000956)__  (__[group A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441835)__ ) and they were __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  with the __[remainder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527428)__  (__[group B](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441836)__ ) for __[complications](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009566)__  after the __[procedure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018795)__  (__[bleeding](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019080)__  and __[vascular access complications](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0920165)__ ). __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  in __[group A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441835)__  were __[older](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1518563)__  (74±12 years vs. 68±17 years, p<0.01) and the main __[indication](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3146298)__  for __[anticoagulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003281)__  was __[atrial fibrillation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004238)__  (58.6%). __[No](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513916)__  __[complications](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009566)__  occurred during the __[procedures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018795)__ . There were __[no](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513916)__  __[acute bleedings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0333276)__  just __[after](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0687676)__  the __[bandage](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004726)__  __[removal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1883720)__ . During the first 24h, only 3 (2.1%) __[radial occlusions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1110554)__  in __[group A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441835)__  and 2 (0.6%) in __[group B](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441836)__  (p=0.14) were __[recorded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2355580)__ . __[Hematomas](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018944)__  between 5 and 10cm appeared in 5% of the __[group A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441835)__  vs. 4.6% in __[group B](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441836)__ . During the __[1-month](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1442451)__  __[follow-up](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522577)__  __[period](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1948053)__ , one more __[radial occlusion](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1110554)__  in each __[group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441833)__  was __[recorded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2355580)__  and there were 4 (1.1%) additional __[mild](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2945599)__  __[hematomas](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0018944)__  in __[group B](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441836)__  and none in __[group A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441835)__  (p=0.48). __[Performing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0884358)__  a __[transradial diagnostic cardiac catheterization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2041518)__  __[without](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332288)__  __[removal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1883720)__  of the __[oral](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0442027)__  __[chronic anticoagulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0694554)__  appears __[safe](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3266157)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  under __[acenocumarol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0000956)__  __[therapy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__ 

* * *

__Does infrared visualization improve selection of venipuncture sites for indwelling needle at the forearm in second-year nursing students?__

Does __[infrared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0181645)__  __[visualization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0234621)__  improve __[selection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707391)__  of __[venipuncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  for __[indwelling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439848)__  __[needle](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027551)__  at the __[forearm](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016536)__  in second-year __[nursing students](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038496)__ ?
To evaluate the __[effectiveness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280519)__  of a __[vein visualization display system](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025080)__  using __[near-infrared light](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1289901)__  (" __[Vein Display](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025080)__  ") for the safe and proper __[selection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707391)__  of __[venipuncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  for __[indwelling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439848)__  __[needle](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027551)__  placement in the __[forearm](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016536)__ . Ten second year __[nursing students](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038496)__  were recruited to apply an __[indwelling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439848)__  __[needle](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027551)__  line with and without __[Vein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042449)__  __[Display](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870432)__ . Another ten __[participants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  were recruited from various __[faculty](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0015535)__  to serve as __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . The quality of the __[venipuncture procedure](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  at various selected __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  was evaluated according to a __[scale](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0349674)__  developed by the __[authors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3812881)__ . __[Time](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040223)__ , __[scores](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449820)__  and __[patterns](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332307)__  of __[puncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  - __[site](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  __[selection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707391)__  were compared with respect to three different methods: [1] attempt 1 (__[tourniquet](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040519)__  only), [2] attempt 2 (__[Vein Display](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025080)__  only) and [3] attempt 3 (both). To validate the __[effectiveness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280519)__  of __[Vein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042449)__  __[Display](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0870432)__ , 52 trials were conducted in total. We found that __[venipuncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  __[site](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__  __[selection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707391)__  time was significantly improved with the __[Vein Display](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025080)__ , particularly in the case of difficult to __[administer](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1621583)__  __[venipuncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  __[sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205145)__ . Overall, we found no significant difference with respect to __[venipuncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__  __[quality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332306)__ , as determined by our __[scale](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0349674)__ . These results suggest that equipment such as the __[Vein Display](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025080)__  can contribute immensely to the improvement of __[practical skills](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008973)__ , such as __[venipuncture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600406)__ , especially in the context of __[elderly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001792)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ 

* * *

__Elective Nephron Sparing Surgery Decreases Other Cause Mortality Relative to Radical Nephrectomy Only in Specific Subgroups of Patients with Renal Cell Carcinoma__

__[Elective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206058)__  __[Nephron Sparing Surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  __[Decreases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205216)__  __[Other Cause Mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__  __[Relative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205345)__  to __[Radical Nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__  Only in __[Specific](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205369)__  __[Subgroups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1515021)__  of __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[Renal Cell Carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007134)__ 
There is no __[consensus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0376298)__  regarding a __[protective effect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1545588)__  on __[mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205848)__  due to a cause other than __[cancer](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006826)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[treated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[elective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206058)__  __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  __[relative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205345)__  to their __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__  counterparts. We __[test](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039593)__  whether the __[protective effect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1545588)__  of __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  __[relative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205345)__  to __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__  is __[universal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0175671)__  or present in __[specific](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205369)__  __[subgroups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1515021)__  of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . A __[collaborative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__  __[database](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242356)__  of 5 __[institutions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1272753)__  was __[queried](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522634)__  to __[evaluate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  1,783 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  without __[chronic kidney disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__  __[diagnosed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  with a __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[T1 renal mass](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2217020)__  that was __[treated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332293)__  __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  or __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__ . __[Multivariable Cox regression analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034980)__  was done to __[assess](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184514)__  the __[impact](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049986)__  of __[surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543467)__  type (__[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  vs __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__ ) on __[other cause mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__  after adjustment for __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  and __[cancer](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006826)__  __[characteristics](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521970)__ . __[Interaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704675)__  terms were used to __[test](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039593)__  the hypothesis that the __[impact](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049986)__  of __[surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0543467)__  type varies according to __[specific](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205369)__  __[subcohorts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599755)__  of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Ten-year](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__  __[other cause mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__  -free __[survival rates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038954)__  were 90% and 88% after __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  and __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__ , respectively. In the __[overall](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561607)__  __[population](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1257890)__  __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__  was not __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  an __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035647)__  of __[other cause mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__  on __[multivariable analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026777)__  compared to __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  (__[HR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2985465)__  0.91, 95% __[CI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009667)__  0.6-1.38, p = 0.6). However, __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__  __[increased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  the __[risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035647)__  of __[other cause mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__  according to the __[increasing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205217)__  __[baseline](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1442488)__  __[Charlson comorbidity index](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714916)__  (__[interaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704675)__  __[test](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039593)__  p = 0.0008). For example, in a __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with a __[Charlson comorbidity index](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714916)__  of 4 the __[probability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033204)__  of __[10-year](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__  __[other cause mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__  -free __[survival](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038952)__  was 86% after __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  and 60% after __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__ . __[Elective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206058)__  __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  does not __[improve](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0184511)__  other cause __[survival](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038952)__  __[relative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205345)__  to __[radical nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0401181)__  consistently in all __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[kidney cancer](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0740457)__ . __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  who are more __[ill](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221423)__  with __[relevant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347946)__  __[comorbidities](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009488)__  are those who __[benefit](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0814225)__  the most from __[nephron sparing surgery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0194086)__  in terms of __[other cause mortality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0476465)__
