__A prime a day keeps calories away: The effects of supraliminal priming on food consumption and the moderating role of gender and eating restraint__

A __[prime](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  a day keeps __[calories](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1556156)__  away: The __[effects of](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704420)__  __[supraliminal priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  on __[food consumption](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2983605)__  and the __[moderating role](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704326)__  of __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__  and __[eating restraint](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0451424)__ 
The link between __[intentions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162425)__  and __[action](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3266814)__  in __[weight control](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0920298)__  is weaker than previously thought, so recent __[research](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035168)__  has called for further investigation of ways to improve __[weight control](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0920298)__  that bypass __[conscious](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0234421)__  __[intentions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162425)__ . __[Priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  has been shown to have effects on individual behavior in a variety of contexts by influencing __[subconscious](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038535)__  __[cognition](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009240)__ . This paper investigates the __[effects of](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704420)__  __[semantic priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871332)__  using __[healthy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3898900)__  __[body image](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005891)__ , __[goal-oriented words](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042926)__  on __[food consumption](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2983605)__ . The __[moderating role](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704326)__  of both __[restrained eating](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0451424)__  and __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__  is investigated. 161 __[participants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  were involved in an __[experiment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681814)__  using a novel version of a scrambled __[sentence](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0876929)__  __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  __[game](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0150593)__ . The outcome measure was the number of __[kilocalories](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439259)__  __[consumed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0513065)__ , examined using a between subjects __[ANCOVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0814908)__  with __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__ , __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__ , __[restrained eating index](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0451424)__ , __[self-reported](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2700446)__  __[BMI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1305855)__ , and two __[interaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704675)__  terms (__[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  x __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__ , and __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  x __[restrained eating index](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0451424)__ ). There was no main __[effect of](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704420)__  __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  but there was an __[interaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704675)__  of __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  with __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__ . __[Females](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086287)__  consumed significantly fewer __[kilocalories](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439259)__  after being exposed to __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  __[words](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042926)__  related to a __[healthy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3898900)__  __[body image](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005891)__  (i.e. "slim", "fit,") compared to __[females](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086287)__  receiving the neutral __[prime](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__ , with a medium effect size (d = 0.58). The __[body image](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005891)__  __[prime](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  did not significantly affect __[food intake](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013470)__  for __[males](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086582)__ , nor did it have a differential effect on __[restrained eaters](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__ . This study shows that __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  can be an effective method for influencing __[females](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086287)__  to reduce __[food intake](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013470)__ , regardless of whether they are __[restrained](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  or __[unrestrained eaters](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__ . Future studies could investigate whether different __[priming](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825344)__  __[words](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042926)__  related to a __[male's](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086582)__  __[healthy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3898900)__  __[body image](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005891)__  goal (i.e. "buff," " __[muscles](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026845)__  ," etc.) would similarly reduce __[food intake](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013470)__  for __[males](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086582)__ 

* * *

__Neurotrophins and specific receptors in the oviduct tracts of Japanese quail (Coturnix coturnix japonica)__

__[Neurotrophins](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__  and __[specific receptors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0254837)__  in the __[oviduct tracts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029954)__  of __[Japanese quail](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022345)__  (__[Coturnix coturnix japonica](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022345)__ )
__[Neurotrophins](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__  (__[NGF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027752)__ , __[BDNF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0107103)__  and __[NT-3](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0083735)__ ) and their __[specific receptors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0254837)__  (__[TrkA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0072482)__ , __[TrkB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0084873)__  and __[TrkC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0132300)__ ) were __[studied](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  in the __[oviduct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029954)__  of __[egg laying](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1622979)__  __[quails](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022345)__ . __[Neurotrophins](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__  (__[NTs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__ ) are mainly involved in the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  and __[maintenance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0587894)__  of __[neuronal populations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027882)__  in the __[central](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714787)__  and __[peripheral nervous system](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206417)__ , but also in __[reproductive system](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1261210)__ . In this survey, we first __[studied](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  the __[morphological](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332437)__  __[organization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029237)__  of the __[quail](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022345)__  __[oviduct](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029954)__ , distinguished in __[infundibulum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0227911)__ , __[magnum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0229962)__ , __[isthmus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0227909)__ , __[uterus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042149)__  and __[vagina](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0042232)__ , and then we __[analyzed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0936012)__  the __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  and __[localization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007613)__  of __[NTs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__  and __[Trks receptors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0254837)__  in the whole __[tracts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029954)__ . By __[western blotting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005863)__  we detected that the __[investigated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__  __[NTs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__  and __[Trks receptors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0254837)__  are __[expressed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  in all __[oviductal tracts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029954)__ . By __[immunohistochemistry](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021044)__  we were able to define the __[distribution](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0872250)__  of __[NTs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027754)__  and __[Trks](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0254837)__ . Specifically, __[NGF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027752)__ , __[BDNF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0107103)__  and __[NT3](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0083735)__  were localized in __[lining](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  and __[ductal epithelial cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512085)__ , and __[NGF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027752)__  was also detected in __[secretory cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1519221)__  of __[tubular glands](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1179446)__  and in __[nervous fibers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027749)__  of __[vessel wall](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0507777)__ . __[TrkA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0072482)__  and __[TrkB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0084873)__  were present in the __[lining](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  and __[ductal epithelium](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512086)__ ; __[TrkA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0072482)__  and __[TrkC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0132300)__  were present in __[nervous fibers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027749)__  of __[vessel wall](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0507777)__  in all __[oviductal tracts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029954)__ . Furthermore, we also observed __[NGF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027752)__  and __[BDNF](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0107103)__  co-localized with __[TrkA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0072482)__  and __[TrkB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0084873)__  in __[cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  of the __[lining](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254362)__  and __[ductal epithelium](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512086)__ , suggesting an __[autocrine mechanism](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3825249)__  of __[action](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3266814)__ 

* * *

__Laser -facilitated epicutaneous immunotherapy to IgE-mediated allergy__

__[Laser](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023089)__  -facilitated __[epicutaneous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001558)__  __[immunotherapy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021083)__  to __[IgE-mediated allergy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1706410)__ 
__[Allergen specific immunotherapy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__  has been shown to be the only __[effective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704419)__  __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  for __[long-lasting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443252)__  __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[benefit](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0814225)__  to __[IgE-mediated allergic diseases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1706410)__ , but a fewer than 5% of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  choose the __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  because of inconvenience and a __[high risk of](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332167)__  __[anaphylaxis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002792)__ . Recently, __[epicutaneous allergen-specific immunotherapy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__  (__[EPIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__ ) has proven __[effective](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704419)__ , yet with __[limitations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449295)__  owing to __[strong skin reactions](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221743)__ . We demonstrate here safer and faster __[EPIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__ , named __[μEPIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__ , by __[delivering](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705822)__  __[powdered allergen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002092)__  and __[adjuvants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001551)__  into many __[micropores](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1325742)__  in the __[epidermis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014520)__ . We fabricated a __[microarray](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1709016)__  __[patch](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0991556)__  fractionally __[coated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522408)__  with a __[powder mixture of ovalbumin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029923)__  (__[OVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029923)__ ) model __[allergen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002092)__ , __[CpG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0056912)__ , and __[1,25-dihydroxyvitamin D3](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006674)__  (__[VD3](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006674)__ ). __[Topical application](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0683174)__  of the __[patch](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0991556)__  onto __[laser-microperforated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1709025)__  __[skin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1123023)__  __[resulted in](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332294)__  a high __[level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  of __[epidermal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014520)__  __[delivery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705822)__  while greatly minimizing __[allergen](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002092)__  __[leakage](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4281748)__  into __[circulation system](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007226)__  as __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  to current __[subcutaneous immunotherapy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0413381)__  (__[SCIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0413381)__ ). Moreover, only three times of __[μEPIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__  over two weeks could sufficiently __[inhibit](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3463820)__  __[allergen-specific IgE](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443736)__  __[responses](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871261)__  in __[mice](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025929)__  suffering __[OVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029923)__  -induced __[airway hyperresponsivness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035228)__  (__[AHR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035228)__ ), which was unattainable by eight times of __[SCIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0413381)__  over three weeks. Mechanistically, __[μEPIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__  preferably __[enhanced](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2349975)__  __[IgG2a](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020857)__  __[production](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003261)__  suggesting __[TH1-biased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242632)__  __[immune responses](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0301872)__  and __[induced](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205263)__  a high __[level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  of __[T-regulatory](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039198)__  (__[Treg](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039198)__ ) __[cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007634)__  against repeated __[allergen sensitization](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2938930)__ . The __[immune tolerance](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020963)__  was __[confirmed by](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521093)__  marked __[reduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441610)__  in __[airway wall](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0458827)__  __[thickness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205400)__  as well as __[eosinophil](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0014467)__  and __[neutrophil infiltration](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0751982)__  into the __[respiratory airway](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282335)__ . The __[μEPIT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162352)__  __[represents](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1882932)__  a __[novel](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205314)__  and __[painless](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0234226)__  __[technology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039421)__  to __[treat](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  __[IgE-mediated allergic diseases](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1706410)__  with little __[local skin reaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221743)__  and a minimal risk of __[anaphylaxis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002792)__ 

* * *

__Predicting real - world functional milestones in schizophrenia__

__[Predicting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681842)__  __[real](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237400)__  - __[world](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2700280)__  __[functional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  __[milestones](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347129)__  in __[schizophrenia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036341)__ 
__[Schizophrenia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036341)__  is a __[severe disorder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1836348)__  that often causes __[impairments](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221099)__  in major areas of __[functioning](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0542341)__ , and most __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  do not achieve expected __[real](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237400)__  - __[world](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2700280)__  __[functional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  __[milestones](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347129)__ . The aim of this __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  was to identify which __[variables](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439828)__  of __[demography](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011298)__ , __[illness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221423)__  __[activity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441655)__ , and __[functional capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1998319)__  predict __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  ' ability to attain __[real](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237400)__  - __[world](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2700280)__  __[functional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  __[milestones](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2347129)__ . __[Participants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0679646)__  were 235 __[outpatients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029921)__ , 149 __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__  and 86 __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__ , __[diagnosed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011900)__  with __[schizophrenia](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0036341)__  __[spectrum disorder](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004936)__ . Our results showed that __[younger](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332239)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  managed to achieve a __[higher](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205250)__  __[level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  of __[functioning](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0542341)__  in __[educational level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013658)__ , __[marital status](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024819)__ , and __[social contacts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__ . __[Patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  ' __[functional capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1998319)__  was primarily associated with __[educational level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013658)__  and __[housing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020056)__  situation. We also found that __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  needed less support regarding __[housing](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0020056)__  and obtained a __[higher](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205250)__  __[level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441889)__  of __[marital status](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024819)__  as compared with __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__ . Our __[findings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  demonstrate the importance of considering __[current](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521116)__  __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__ , especially __[negative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205160)__  __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__ , and __[remission](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0544452)__  __[stability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205360)__  over __[time](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040223)__ , together with __[age](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__ , __[duration of illness](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3176590)__ , __[gender](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__ , __[educational level](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013658)__ , and __[current](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0521116)__  __[functional capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1998319)__ , when predicting __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  ' future __[real](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0237400)__  - __[world](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2700280)__  __[functioning](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0542341)__ . We also conclude that there is an advantage in exploring __[symptoms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1457887)__  divided into __[positive](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1446409)__ , __[negative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205160)__ , and general domains considering their probable __[impact](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049986)__  on __[functional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  __[achievements](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001072)__ 

* * *

__LDLR, ApoB and ApoE genes polymorphisms and classical risk factors in premature coronary artery disease__

__[LDLR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__ , __[ApoB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  and __[ApoE genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  and classical __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  in __[premature coronary artery disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__ 
__[Lipoproteins](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023820)__  play a central role in the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[atherosclerotic disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004153)__ . So, with their ability to affect __[lipid levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0428460)__ , the __[LDLR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__ , __[ApoB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  and __[ApoE](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  could be one of the factors influencing __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[atherosclerosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0004153)__ . This __[hypothesis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512571)__  has been __[tested](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392366)__  in different __[populations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032659)__  with conflicting results. The purpose of the present study was to __[investigate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__  the association between the __[LDLR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__ , __[ApoB](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  and __[ApoE genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  with __[premature CAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  (__[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__ ) in __[Egyptians](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0337801)__ . One hundred thirty-five __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  of __[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  and one hundred thirty-two __[ages](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001779)__  and __[sex](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522384)__  matched control subjects were included in the study. __[LDLR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  and __[ApoB genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  were __[analyzed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0936012)__  by __[polymerase chain reaction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032520)__  (__[PCR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032520)__ ). The __[ApoE](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[genotypes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__  were identified by __[multiplex amplification refractory mutation system](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2732542)__  (__[multi-AMRS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2732542)__ ). We found that __[LDLR A(+)A(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  __[genotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__ , __[ApoB X(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  and __[ApoE E4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  increased the risk of __[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  by 1.8, 2.1 and 12.1 respectively. The present study proved that __[smoking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037369)__ , __[metabolic syndrome](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0524620)__ , __[ApoB X(+)X(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  __[genotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__  and __[ApoE E4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  were independent __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  for the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__ . This is the first study __[investigate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1292732)__  the association between __[low density lipoprotein receptor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__ , __[apolipoprotein B](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  and __[apolipoprotein E genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[polymorphisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0678951)__  with __[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  and __[lipid levels](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0428460)__  in __[Egyptians](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0337801)__  and we concluded that the __[LDLR A(+)A(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  __[genotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__ , __[ApoB X(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  and __[ApoE E4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  may be __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  an increased risk for __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  by elevated __[levels of total cholesterol (TC)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0201950)__  and __[low density lipoprotein](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0202116)__  (__[LDLc](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0202116)__ ). The coexistence of __[CAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  with __[LDLR A(+)A(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1366529)__  __[genotype](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017431)__ , __[ApoB X(+)](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412471)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  and __[ApoE E4](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1412481)__  __[allele](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0002085)__  may increase the risk of the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[PCAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1867743)__  in __[Egyptian](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0337801)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__
