__The influence of liposomal formulation on the incorporation and retention of PNA oligomers__

The influence of __[liposomal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023828)__  __[formulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705957)__  on the __[incorporation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243126)__  and __[retention](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0333117)__  of __[PNA oligomers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600500)__ 
__[Liposomal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023828)__  __[formulations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705957)__  composed of __[phospholipids](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031676)__  with different __[unsaturation degrees](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522535)__ , __[head groups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  and at different __[cholesterol content have been tested](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0201950)__  for the __[encapsulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348438)__  of __[Peptide Nucleic Acid (PNA) oligomers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600500)__ . The __[best loading capability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3714444)__  (177μg, __[ER](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0456603)__  %=87.2) was obtained for pure __[liposomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023828)__  of __[phosphatidylglycerol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043840)__  (__[DOPG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043840)__ ) with __[negatively charged](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0003075)__  __[head group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__ . The __[insertion](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441587)__  of a 10-20% of __[cholesterol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008377)__  in __[DOPG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043840)__  based __[liposomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023828)__  provides a slight __[decrease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547047)__  (∼160μg) of the __[PNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600500)__  __[loading](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1708715)__ . On the other hand, the __[cholesterol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008377)__  __[addition](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1524062)__  (20-30%) slows down the __[PNA's](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600500)__  __[release](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3850077)__  (∼27%) in __[fetal bovine serum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3812213)__  from the __[liposomal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023828)__  __[formulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705957)__ . Based on the __[encapsulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348438)__  and the __[release properties](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3850077)__ , __[PEGylated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032483)__  __[DOPG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043840)__  __[liposomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0023828)__  with a percentage of __[cholesterol](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008377)__  of 10-20% are the __[optimal formulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0524527)__  for the __[loading](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1708715)__  of __[PNA-a210](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600500)__ 

* * *

__Mandibular kinesiographic pattern of women with chronic TMD after management with educational and self-care therapies: A double-blind, randomized clinical trial__

__[Mandibular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024687)__  __[kinesiographic pattern](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282574)__  of __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  with __[chronic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205191)__  __[TMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039494)__  after __[management](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0376636)__  with __[educational](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013622)__  and __[self-care therapies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0567459)__ : A __[double-blind](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013072)__ , __[randomized clinical trial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206034)__ 
__[Limited mandibular movements](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4228933)__  are one of the most __[important](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3898777)__  __[signs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037088)__  of __[temporomandibular disorders](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039494)__  (__[TMDs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039494)__ ) and may __[cause](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0015127)__  __[functional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205245)__  __[difficulties](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332218)__ . The purpose of this __[double-blind](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013072)__ , __[randomized clinical trial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0206034)__  was to __[evaluate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  the __[effect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280500)__  of __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  with only __[educational](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013622)__  or __[education](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013622)__  __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  __[self-care therapies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0567459)__  on the __[pattern](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282574)__  of __[mandibular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024687)__  __[movements](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  of __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  with __[chronic painful](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0150055)__  __[TMDs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039494)__ . __[Forty-two](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__  __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  were __[selected](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707391)__  and __[randomly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439605)__  __[divided](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332849)__  into 3 __[groups](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__ , __[control group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009932)__  (__[CG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009932)__ , n=13), __[education group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  (__[EG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__ , n=16), and __[education and self-care group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  (__[ESG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__ , n=13), according to the __[sequence](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1519249)__  of __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  they __[received](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514756)__ . A __[kinesiograph device](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025080)__  __[recorded](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2355580)__  __[mandibular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024687)__  __[movements](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  __[during](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0347984)__  __[maximum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0806909)__  __[mouth](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0226896)__  __[opening](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  and __[mastication](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024888)__  at __[baseline](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1442488)__  (__[T0](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__ ) and at __[30-day](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  (__[T1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__ ) and __[60-day](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  (__[T2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__ ) __[follow-up](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522577)__ . __[Kinesiographic data](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1516606)__  were __[statistically analyzed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0871424)__  __[using](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1524063)__  __[1-way ANOVA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1709320)__ , __[followed by](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332283)__  the __[Bonferroni test](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1879894)__  for __[multiple](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439064)__  __[comparisons](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  of __[means](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704970)__  (α=.05). The __[ESG group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  demonstrated an __[improvement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2986411)__  in the __[maximum vertical opening](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  (__[MVO](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  = 5.1 ±3.4 mm; P=.012) and __[anteroposterior mandibular movement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  (__[MAM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__ ) __[during](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0347984)__  __[maximum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0806909)__  __[opening](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  (7.4 ±9.5; P=.019), __[significantly higher](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4055637)__  than that of the __[EG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  (__[MVO](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  =1.8 ±3.5 mm; __[MAM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  =0.8 ±5.0 mm) and the __[CG](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009932)__  (__[MVO](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  =0.9 ±3.8 mm; __[MAM](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  =0.8 ±4.4 mm) after __[30 days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  of __[follow-up](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522577)__ . Moreover, at __[T1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1254367)__ , __[vertical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205128)__  __[mandibular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024687)__  __[movement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  __[during](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0347984)__  __[mastication](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024888)__  was __[significantly higher](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4055637)__  in the __[ESG group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  (17.4 ±1.7 mm) than in the __[EG group](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0681860)__  (15.0 ±2.8, P=.027). __[No significant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1273937)__  __[differences](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1705242)__  were __[found](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0150312)__  between the __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  who __[received](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514756)__  __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  with __[educational](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013622)__  and __[self-care therapies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0567459)__  for __[60 days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__  and the __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  who __[received](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514756)__  this __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  for __[30 days](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439228)__ . In the __[short-term](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443303)__ , __[education](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013622)__  and __[self-care treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0567459)__  __[positively](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1446409)__  __[influenced](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4054723)__  the __[mandibular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024687)__  __[movement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026649)__  __[pattern](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0282574)__  of __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  with __[chronic painful](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0150055)__  __[TMDs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0039494)__ 

* * *

__Histopathology of the filum terminale in children with and without tethered cord syndrome with attention to the elastic tissue within the filum__

__[Histopathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0677043)__  of the __[filum terminale](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  in __[children](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0008059)__  with and __[without](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332288)__  __[tethered cord syndrome](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__  with attention to the __[elastic tissue](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013762)__  within the __[filum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__ 
To __[compare](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  __[histologically](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205462)__  __[transected](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332847)__  __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  from __[pediatric](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521725)__  __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[tethered cord syndrome](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__  (__[TCS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__ ), with and __[without](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332288)__  a __[low](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1548802)__  __[conus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0149601)__ , with controls, focusing on __[collagenous](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0225333)__  and __[elastic tissue](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013762)__ . Thirty __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  from __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[TCS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__ , including 5 where __[minimal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547040)__  __[cautery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007471)__  was used prior to __[filum](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  __[section](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0700320)__ , were __[compared](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707455)__  with __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  from 27 __[pediatric](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521725)__  __[cadavers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006629)__  __[without](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332288)__  __[TCS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__  (__[controls](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009932)__ ). __[Sections](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522472)__  of __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  were __[stained](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0487602)__  with __[H&E](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0523207)__ , __[Masson trichrome](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1294297)__  and __[Verhoeff von Gieson elastic stains](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1294321)__ , and 7 with __[Gordon and Sweet's reticulin stain](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1293950)__ . __[Fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  from __[controls](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009932)__  showed __[loose](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205407)__  __[fibrous connective tissue](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1184823)__  (__[FCT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1184823)__ ) with __[thin](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205168)__  and __[evenly dispersed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704711)__  __[elastic fibers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__  (__[EFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__ ). __[Reticulin fibers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035285)__  (__[RFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035285)__ ) were seen in __[blood vessel walls](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1180033)__  and __[nerve](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027740)__  twigs. __[Fat](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0015677)__  was __[identified](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205396)__  __[microscopically](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205288)__  in 2 __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__ . All __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  from __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[TCS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__  had __[dense FCT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0225333)__ . The __[EFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__  were in __[normal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205307)__  numbers in 17, and __[focally](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205234)__  or __[diffusely](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332261)__  __[decreased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205216)__  in 13. All 25 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  where the __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  were __[cauterized](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007471)__  during __[resection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728940)__  had __[thick](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280412)__  and __[coiled](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1880179)__  __[EFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__ . __[Coiling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0444764)__  was not seen when __[minimal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0547040)__  __[cautery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007471)__  was applied. __[RFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035285)__  were seen in __[blood vessel walls](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1180033)__  and nerve twigs. __[Fat](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0015677)__  was __[identified](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205396)__  in 19 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Findings](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0243095)__  were __[similar](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348205)__ , whether the __[conus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0149601)__  termination was __[normal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205307)__  or __[low](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441994)__ . The __[fila](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016109)__  of all __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[TCS](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0080218)__ , whether or not the __[conus](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0149601)__  was __[low](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441994)__ , showed __[abnormal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205161)__  __[FCT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1184823)__ . __[EFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__  were __[decreased](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205216)__  in 48 % of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ ; however, there were __[thick](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280412)__  and __[coiled](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1880179)__  __[EFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__  in all __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Coiling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0444764)__  of __[EFs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0230899)__ , initially thought to be an __[abnormality](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1704258)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ , is considered most likely to be a __[result](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0808233)__  of __[cautery](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007471)__  (i.e., __[artifactual](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085089)__  / __[iatrogenic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439669)__  __[coiling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0444764)__ 

* * *

__Clinical value of pathologic examination of non-neoplastic kidney in patients with upper urinary tract malignancies__

__[Clinical value](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2826293)__  of __[pathologic examination](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4086729)__  of __[non-neoplastic kidney](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  in __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[upper urinary tract](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1278977)__  __[malignancies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__ 
While __[surgical resection](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0728940)__  remains the standard of __[care](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1947933)__  in the __[treatment](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0087111)__  of __[upper urinary tract](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1278977)__  __[malignancies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__ , __[nephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027695)__  is a __[risk factor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  for the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[chronic kidney disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__  (__[CKD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__ ). The aim of this __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__  was to determine whether __[histologic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205462)__  __[evaluation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  of __[non-neoplastic kidney](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  could enable __[early identification](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0814435)__  of unrecognized __[kidney disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022658)__  and could be of __[prognostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220901)__  value in predicting __[postoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032790)__  __[renal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  __[outcomes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085415)__ . We __[retrospectively analyzed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035363)__  51 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  with __[upper urinary tract](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1278977)__  __[malignancies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4282132)__  who received __[uninephrectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027695)__  or __[uninephroureterectomy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027732)__ . A thorough __[pathologic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521733)__  __[evaluation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  of __[non-neoplastic kidney](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  including __[special stains](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2038188)__ , __[immunofluorescence](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079603)__ , and __[electron microscopic studies](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026019)__  was performed. The __[degree](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449286)__  of __[parenchymal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0933845)__  __[changes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392747)__  was graded from 0 to 15. Of 51 __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ , only 13 showed normal __[kidney](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  __[pathology](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030664)__ . Fifteen __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  showed __[glomerular abnormalities](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1398788)__ , 14 showed __[diabetic nephropathy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0011881)__ , and 11 showed __[vascular](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005847)__  __[nephropathy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027695)__ . There was one case each of __[reflux nephropathy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3495566)__  and __[chronic pyelonephritis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085697)__ . The median __[histologic score](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449820)__  was 5 points. Only 25.4% of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  had ≤ 3 points. __[Score](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0449820)__  more than 5 was observed in 47.1% of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Postoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032790)__  __[estimated glomerular filtration rate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3811844)__  (__[eGFR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3811844)__ ) at 3 to 36 __[months](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439231)__  were obtained from 90.2% of __[patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ , and of those, 34.8% had de novo __[CKD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__ . Since no one had __[CKD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__  in partial __[nephrectomized patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ , we determined __[risk factors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035648)__  for __[CKD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__  in radical __[nephrectomized patients](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__ . __[Cox regression analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0034980)__  revealed that __[postoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0032790)__  __[AKI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2609414)__ , __[preoperative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0445204)__  __[eGFR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3811844)__ , and __[histologic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205462)__  score of __[non-neoplastic kidney](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  were the independent __[predictors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2698872)__  for __[CKD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1561643)__ . We conclude that routine __[pathologic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521733)__  __[evaluation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220825)__  of __[non-neoplastic kidney](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0022646)__  provides valuable __[diagnostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0348026)__  and __[prognostic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220901)__ 

* * *

__Prospective study of dietary Non Enzymatic Antioxidant Capacity on the risk of hip fracture in the elderly__

Prospective study of __[dietary](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012155)__  __[Non Enzymatic Antioxidant Capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  on the __[risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035647)__  of __[hip fracture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019557)__  in the __[elderly](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0001792)__ 
__[Dietary antioxidants](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0729311)__  may play an important role in the prevention of __[bone loss](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0029453)__  and associated __[fractures](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0016658)__  by reducing levels of __[oxidative stress](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242606)__ . We prospectively investigated the association between __[dietary](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012155)__  __[Non Enzymatic Antioxidant Capacity](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  (__[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__ ) and the __[risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035647)__  of __[hip fracture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019557)__  and whether this effect was modified by __[smoking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037369)__ . In the __[Swedish National March Cohort](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0599755)__  13,409 __[men](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025266)__  and __[women](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0043210)__  over the age of 55 who had not experienced __[cancer](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006826)__ , __[cardiovascular disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007222)__  or __[hip fracture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019557)__ , were followed through __[record-linkages](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025101)__  from 1997 through 2010. __[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  was assessed by a validated __[food frequency questionnaire](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2986698)__  collected at __[baseline](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1442488)__ . We categorized the distribution of __[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  into __[sex](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079399)__  - __[specific](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205369)__  __[quartiles](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2828255)__  and used __[multivariable adjusted Cox proportional hazards regression models](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033489)__  to estimate __[hazard ratios](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2985465)__  (__[HRs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2985465)__ ) with 95% __[confidence intervals](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009667)__  (95% __[CI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009667)__ ). During a mean __[follow-up](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1522577)__  __[time](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040223)__  of 12.4years, we identified 491 incident cases of first __[hip fracture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019557)__ . Subjects in the highest __[quartile](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2828255)__  of __[dietary](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012155)__  __[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  had a 39% __[lower risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3843763)__  of incident __[hip fracture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019557)__  compared to those in the lowest __[quartile](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2828255)__  (__[HR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2985465)__ : 0.61; 95% __[CI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009667)__ : 0.44-0.85). The association was non-linear (p for non-linearity: 0.004) with a potential threshold between the first and the second __[quartile](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2828255)__  and no further __[risk reduction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1137094)__  at higher levels of __[dietary](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012155)__  __[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__ . Due to a low smoking prevalence in our study population, we had limited power to detect effect modification between __[dietary](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012155)__  __[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  and __[smoking](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0037369)__  on a __[multiplicative](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2911648)__  or __[additive scale](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0392762)__ . Higher dietary __[NEAC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4049177)__  intake is associated with lower __[risk](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035647)__  of __[hip fracture](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019557)__ 

* * *

__MiR-211 is epigenetically regulated by DNMT1 mediated methylation and inhibits EMT of melanoma cells by targeting RAB22A__

__[MiR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  is __[epigenetically regulated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1160454)__  by __[DNMT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414121)__  mediated __[methylation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025723)__  and __[inhibits](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3463820)__  __[EMT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1523298)__  of __[melanoma cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513095)__  by __[targeting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242613)__  __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__ 
__[MiR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  has strong __[inhibitive](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3463820)__  effects on __[melanoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025202)__  __[cell growth](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0007595)__ , __[invasion](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2699153)__  and __[metastasis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4255448)__ . However, how it is __[downregulated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013081)__  and whether other __[genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017337)__  are involved its __[downstream](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0522506)__  __[regulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013081)__  in __[melanoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025202)__  are not clear. In this study, we firstly verified the __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  of __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  in __[melanoma cell lines](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513095)__  and observed that its __[downregulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013081)__  is __[associated with](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0332281)__  increased __[DNMT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414121)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__ . By performing __[qRT-PCR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514628)__  and __[MSP analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0026031)__ , we confirmed that __[DNMT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414121)__  is __[negatively](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513916)__  __[correlated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1707520)__  with __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__  and can __[modulate](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443264)__  __[DNA methylation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0376452)__  in the __[promoter region](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033413)__  of __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__ . By performing __[bioinformatics analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1140694)__ , we found that __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__  is a possible __[target](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1521840)__  of __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__ , which has two broadly __[conversed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009802)__  __[binding sites](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005456)__  with __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  in the __[3'UTR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0600600)__ . Following dual __[luciferase](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0024075)__  __[assay](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0005507)__ , __[qRT-PCR](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514628)__  and __[western blot analysis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0949466)__  confirmed the direct __[binding](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1167622)__  between __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  and __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__  and the __[suppressive effect](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038855)__  of __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  on __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0017262)__ . __[Knockdown](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2350567)__  of __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__  increased __[epithelial](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221908)__  properties and __[impaired](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0221099)__  __[mesenchymal](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513143)__  properties of the __[melanoma cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513095)__ , suggesting that __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  __[modulates](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443264)__  __[epithelial mesenchymal transition](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1523298)__  (__[EMT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1523298)__ ) of __[melanoma cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1513095)__  via __[downregulating](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013081)__  __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__ . In summary, the present study firstly demonstrated that __[DNMT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414121)__  mediated __[promoter](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033413)__  __[methylation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025723)__  is a __[mechanism](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441712)__  of __[miRNA](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1101610)__  __[suppression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0038855)__  in __[melanoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025202)__  and revealed a new __[tumor suppressor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079427)__  role of the __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  by __[targeting](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242613)__  __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__  in __[melanoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025202)__ . The __[DNMT1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414121)__  / __[miR-211](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1537847)__  / __[RAB22A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1419193)__  axis provides a novel insight into the __[pathogenesis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0699748)__  of __[melanoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0025202)__ , particularly in the __[EMT process](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1523298)__ 

* * *

__Concordant but Varied Phenotypes among Duchenne Muscular Dystrophy Patient -Specific Myoblasts Derived using a Human iPSC -Based Model__

Concordant but Varied __[Phenotypes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  among __[Duchenne Muscular Dystrophy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__  __[Patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  -Specific __[Myoblasts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596995)__  Derived using a __[Human](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086418)__  __[iPSC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2717959)__  -Based __[Model](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0684309)__ 
__[Duchenne muscular dystrophy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__  (__[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__ ) remains an intractable __[genetic disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0019247)__ . Althogh there are several __[animal models](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012644)__  of __[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__ , there is no __[human cell](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0682523)__  model that carries __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  -specific __[DYSTROPHIN](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1414083)__  __[mutations](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596611)__ . Here, we present a __[human](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086418)__  __[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__  __[model](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0684309)__  using __[human induced pluripotent stem cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3658289)__  (__[hiPSCs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3658289)__ ). Our model reveals concordant __[disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012634)__  - __[related](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1552599)__  __[phenotypes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  with __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  - __[dependent](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0851827)__  __[variation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205419)__ , which are partially reversed by __[genetic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0314603)__  and __[pharmacological](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205464)__  approaches. Our " __[chemical-compound](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0220806)__  -based" __[strategy](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0035171)__  successfully directs __[hiPSCs](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3658289)__  into expandable __[myoblasts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596995)__ , which exhibit a __[myogenic transcriptional](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040649)__  __[program](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3484370)__ , forming __[striated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205364)__  __[contractile](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1752744)__  __[myofibers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3179197)__  and participating in __[muscle regeneration](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1850849)__  __[in vivo](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1515655)__ . __[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__  - __[hiPSC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3658289)__  -derived __[myoblasts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596995)__  show __[disease](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0012634)__  - __[related](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1552599)__  __[phenotypes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0031437)__  with __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  -to- __[patient](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0030705)__  __[variability](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2827666)__ , including __[aberrant](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0443127)__  expression of __[inflammation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0021368)__  or __[immune-response genes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086344)__  and __[collagens](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0009325)__ , increased __[BMP](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1155364)__  / __[TGFβ signaling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1155363)__ , and reduced fusion competence. Furthermore, by __[genetic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0314603)__  __[correction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1947976)__  and __[pharmacological](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205464)__  "dual- __[SMAD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1571580)__  " __[inhibition](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1519312)__ , the __[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__  - __[hiPSC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3658289)__  -derived __[myoblasts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596995)__  and __[genetically](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0314603)__  corrected __[isogenic](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2348628)__  __[myoblasts](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0596995)__  form "rescued" __[multi](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0439064)__  - __[nucleated](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1979936)__  __[myotubes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0242697)__ . In conclusion, our findings demonstrate the feasibility of establishing a __[human](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0086418)__  " __[DMD](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013264)__  -in-a-dish" __[model](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0684309)__  using __[hiPSC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3658289)__  -based __[disease modeling](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0684309)__ 

* * *

__SNAI1 promotes the development of HCC through the enhancement of proliferation and inhibition of apoptosis__

__[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  __[promotes](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033414)__  the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[HCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__  through the __[enhancement](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2349975)__  of __[proliferation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514485)__  and __[inhibition of apoptosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1512772)__ 
__[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__ , a __[zinc-finger transcription factor](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040648)__ , plays an important role in the __[induction](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205263)__  of __[epithelial-mesenchymal transition](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1523298)__  (__[EMT](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1523298)__ ) in various __[cancers](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0006826)__ . However, the possible functions of __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  in the __[proliferation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514485)__  and __[apoptosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162638)__  of __[hepatocellular carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__  have not been clearly identified. In this __[study](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2603343)__ , we investigated the __[effects](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1280500)__  and __[mechanisms](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0441712)__  of __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  in the __[proliferation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514485)__  and __[apoptosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162638)__  of __[hepatocellular carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__  using __[clinical](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0205210)__  __[samples](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0370003)__  and __[cell lines](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085983)__ . We found that __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  is highly __[expressed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  in the __[tissues](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040300)__  of __[liver cancer](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__  compared with adjacent __[nontumor tissues](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0040300)__ . __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  is also highly __[expressed](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  in the __[hepatoma cell lines HepG2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2717940)__ , __[SMMC-7721](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085983)__ , and __[BEL-7402](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0085983)__  compared with the __[human normal liver cell line L02](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0682523)__ . We also observed that __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  was correlated with __[distal metastasis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4255448)__ , incomplete __[tumor capsule formation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0027671)__ , and __[histological differentiation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1511938)__  in __[hepatocellular carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__  (__[HCC](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__ ). Moreover, we demonstrated that __[knockdown](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2350567)__  of __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1420267)__  via __[lentiviral](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079679)__  __[vectors](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1520007)__  of __[RNAi](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1136031)__  against __[SNAI](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  inhibited __[cell proliferation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1514485)__  by inducing __[G1 arrest](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C3178834)__ , which was accompanied by the __[downregulation](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0013081)__  of __[cyclin D1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0174680)__  but not that of __[cyclin A](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0079184)__ . In addition, __[knockdown](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2350567)__  of __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1420267)__  __[promoted](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0033414)__  __[apoptosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162638)__  by decreasing the __[expression](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1171362)__  of __[Bcl-2](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4042483)__ . In conclusion, our findings revealed that __[SNAI1](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C4308198)__  is involved in the __[development](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1527148)__  of __[hepatocellular carcinoma](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C2239176)__  via __[regulating the growth](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C1160191)__  and __[apoptosis](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0162638)__  of __[tumor cells](https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/umls/concept/C0597032)__ 

* * *
